Hard or soft, shrill or harmonious, classic or capricious. \r\nA midi file is a collection of sheet music for a whole orchestra with up to 16 voices (= instruments or sounds). PhotoOrganiser shows adds, which will be removed after purchasing.\r\nPhotoOrganiser is never feature-limited .\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\nSummary\r\nPhotoOrganiser lets you view your collection of photos in various ways. To do so it must first import the photo albums from its original source. You can do this in the Import Album page. The source can be any album from the device (mobile or desktop), Picasa web albums or your OneDrive account. During the import, thumbnails and metadata (location, keywords, rating) will be read from the original photos and stored on the device. The metadata can then be used to filter, search, group and order the photos on a variety of ways. During the import, the original photos stay untouched. Photos with a location (latitude, longitude) attached will get a country tag, based on the location, so the pictures can be grouped by country.\r\n\r\nNote that this app assumes that your photos already contain embedded metadata like location, rating and keywords. If not, the advanced search and filter capabilities cannot be exploited to its full strength, but you can still use it as nice photo viewer. To add or edit metadata to the original photos, you must use other applications.\r\n\r\nOnce the albums are imported, you can view the photos in the albums in different ways. The imported albums can be viewed in the Albums page. You can order the albums by Name, Date or Photo source. The photos in the album can be viewed directly by clicking/tapping on the album. However, to use this app to its full potential you should use the Search Photos page. This page offers you an advanced way to view exactly those photos that match the filter criteria that you provide. You can search your photos across all albums and across all photo sources. The photos are ordered and grouped by either Country, Date, Rating or Orientation. You can narrow down the photos to be seen by using different filter criteria. The filter criteria can be created by using different combinations of Date, Country, Keywords (tags), Rating and Orientation and by using operators like =, ≠, ≦ or ≧. The requested photos are shown instantly. Multiple filter commands can be used that will be “stacked” so that subsequent filter commands are accomplished to the filter commands already executed.
